148→// checks if the required cgroups subsystems are mounted.\n   149→// As of now, only 'cpu' and 'memory' are required.\n   150→// cpu quota is a soft requirement.\n   151→func validateSystemRequirements(logger klog.Logger, mountUtil mount.Interface) (features, error) {\n   152→\tconst (\n   153→\t\tcgroupMountType = \"cgroup\"\n   154→\t\tlocalErr        = \"system validation failed\"\n   155→\t)\n   156→\tvar (\n   157→\t\tcpuMountPoint string\n   158→\t\tf             features\n   159→\t)\n   160→\tmountPoints, err := mountUtil.List()\n   161→\tif err != nil {\n   162→\t\treturn f, fmt.Errorf(\"%s - %v\", localErr, err)\n   163→\t}\n   164→\n   165→\tif cgroups.IsCgroup2UnifiedMode() {\n   166→\t\tf.cpuHardcapping = true\n   167→\t\treturn f, nil\n   168→\t}\n   169→\n   170→\texpectedCgroups := sets.New(\"cpu\", \"cpuacct\", \"cpuset\", \"memory\")\n   171→\tfor _, mountPoint := range mountPoints {\n   172→\t\tif mountPoint.Type == cgroupMountType {\n   173→\t\t\tfor _, opt := range mountPoint.Opts {\n   174→\t\t\t\tif expectedCgroups.Has(opt) {\n   175→\t\t\t\t\texpectedCgroups.Delete(opt)\n   176→\t\t\t\t}\n   177→\t\t\t\tif opt == \"cpu\" {\n   178→\t\t\t\t\tcpuMountPoint = mountPoint.Path\n   179→\t\t\t\t}\n   180→\t\t\t}\n   181→\t\t}\n   182→\t}\n   183→\n   184→\tif expectedCgroups.Len() > 0 {\n   185→\t\treturn f, fmt.Errorf(\"%s - Following Cgroup subsystem not mounted: %v\", localErr, sets.List(expectedCgroups))\n   186→\t}\n   187→\n   188→\t// Check if cpu quota is available.\n   189→\t// CPU cgroup is required and so it expected to be mounted at this point.\n   190→\tperiodExists, err := utilpath.Exists(utilpath.CheckFollowSymlink, path.Join(cpuMountPoint, \"cpu.cfs_period_us\"))\n   191→\tif err != nil {\n   192→\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Failed to detect if CPU cgroup cpu.cfs_period_us is available\")\n   193→\t}\n   194→\tquotaExists, err := utilpath.Exists(utilpath.CheckFollowSymlink, path.Join(cpuMountPoint, \"cpu.cfs_quota_us\"))\n   195→\tif err != nil {\n   196→\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Failed to detect if CPU cgroup cpu.cfs_quota_us is available\")\n   197→\t}\n   198→\tif quotaExists && periodExists {\n   199→\t\tf.cpuHardcapping = true\n   200→\t}\n   201→\treturn f, nil\n   202→}\n   203→\n   204→// TODO(vmarmol): Add limits to the system containers.\n   205→// Takes the absolute name of the specified containers.\n   206→// Empty container name disables use of the specified container.\n   207→func NewContainerManager(ctx context.Context, mountUtil mount.Interface, cgroup container manager.\n   435→func createManager(containerName string) (cgroups.Manager, error) {\n   436→\tcg := &cgroups.Cgroup{\n   437→\t\tParent: \"/\",\n   438→\t\tName:   containerName,\n   439→\t\tResources: &cgroups.Resources{\n   440→\t\t\tSkipDevices: true,\n   441→\t\t},\n   442→\t\tSystemd: false,\n   443→\t}\n   444→\n   445→\treturn manager.New(cg)\n   446→}\n   447→\n   448→type KernelTunableBehavior string\n   449→\n   450→const (\n   451→\tKernelTunableWarn   KernelTunableBehavior = \"warn\"\n   452→\tKernelTunableError  KernelTunableBehavior = \"error\"\n   453→\tKernelTunableModify KernelTunableBehavior = \"modify\"\n   454→)\n   455→\n   456→// setupKernelTunables validates kernel tunable flags are set as expected\n   457→// depending upon the specified option, it will either warn, error, or modify the kernel tunable flags\n   458→func setupKernelTunables(logger klog.Logger, option KernelTunableBehavior) error {\n   459→\tdesiredState := map[string]int{\n   460→\t\tutilsysctl.VMOvercommitMemory: utilsysctl.VMOvercommitMemoryAlways,\n   461→\t\tutilsysctl.VMPanicOnOOM:       utilsysctl.VMPanicOnOOMInvokeOOMKiller,\n   462→\t\tutilsysctl.KernelPanic:        utilsysctl.KernelPanicRebootTimeout,\n   463→\t\tutilsysctl.KernelPanicOnOops:  utilsysctl.KernelPanicOnOopsAlways,\n   464→\t\tutilsysctl.RootMaxKeys:        utilsysctl.RootMaxKeysSetting,\n   465→\t\tutilsysctl.RootMaxBytes:       utilsysctl.RootMaxBytesSetting,\n   466→\t}\n   467→\n   468→\tsysctl := utilsysctl.New()\n   469→\n   470→\terrList := []error{}\n   471→\tfor flag, expectedValue := range desiredState {\n   472→\t\tval, err := sysctl.GetSysctl(flag)\n   473→\t\tif err != nil {\n   474→\t\t\terrList = append(errList, err)\n   475→\t\t\tcontinue\n   476→\t\t}\n   477→\t\tif val == expectedValue {\n   478→\t\t\tcontinue\n   479→\t\t}\n   480→\n   481→\t\tswitch option {\n   482→\t\tcase KernelTunableError:\n   483→\t\t\terrList = append(errList, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid kernel flag: %v, expected value: %v, actual value: %v\", flag, expectedValue, val))\n   484→\t\tcase KernelTunableWarn:\n   485→\t\t\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Invalid kernel flag\", \"flag\", flag, \"expectedValue\", expectedValue, \"actualValue\", val)\n   486→\t\tcase KernelTunableModify:\n   487→\t\t\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Updating kernel flag\", \"flag\", flag, \"expectedValue\", expectedValue, \"actualValue\", val)\n   488→\t\t\terr = sysctl.SetSysctl(flag, expectedValue)\n   489→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   490→\t\t\t\tif inuserns.RunningInUserNS() {\n   491→\t\t\t\t\tif utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(kubefeatures.KubeletInUserNamespace) {\n   492→\t\t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Updating kernel flag failed (running in UserNS, ignoring)\", \"flag\", flag, \"err\", err)\n   493→\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   494→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   495→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Updating kernel flag failed (Hint: enable KubeletInUserNamespace feature flag to ignore the error)\", \"flag\", flag)\n   496→\t\t\t\t}\n   497→\t\t\t\terrList = append(errList, err)\n   498→\t\t\t}\n   499→\t\t}\n   500→\t}\n   501→\treturn utilerrors.NewAggregate(errList)\n   502→}\n   503→\n   504→func (cm *containerManagerImpl) setupNode(ctx int(cm.KubeletOOMScoreAdj), nil); err != nil {\n   567→\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Failed to ensure process in container with oom score\")\n   568→\t\t\t\treturn\n   569→\t\t\t}\n   570→\t\t\tcont, 583→\treturn nil\n   584→}\n   585→\n   586→func (cm *containerManagerImpl) GetNodeConfig() NodeConfig {\n   587→\tcm.RLock()\n   588→\tdefer cm.RUnlock()\n   589→\treturn cm.NodeConfig\n   590→}\n 676→\t\t\thasEnsureStateFuncs = true\n   677→\t\t\tbreak\n   678→\t\t}\n   679→\t}\n   680→\tif hasEnsureStateFuncs {\n   681→\t\t// Run ensure state functions every minute.\n   682→\t\tgo {\n   686→\t\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Failed to ensure state\", \"containerName\", cont.name, \"err\", err)\n   687→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   688→\t\t\t\t}\n   689→\t\t\t}\n   690→\t\t}, time.Minute, wait.NeverStop)\n   691→\n   692→\t}\n   693→\n   694→\tif len(cm.periodicTasks) > 0 {\n   695→\t\tgo wait.Until(func() {\n   696→\t\t\tfor _, task := range cm.periodicTasks {\n   697→\t\t\t\tif task != nil {\n   698→\t\t\t\t\ttask()\n   699→\t\t\t\t}\n   700→\t\t\t}\n   701→\t\t}, 5*time.Minute, wait.NeverStop)\n   702→\t}\n   703→\n   704→\t// Starts device manager.\n   705→\tif err := cm.deviceManager.Start(klog.FromContext(ctx), devicemanager.ActivePodsFunc(activePods), sourcesReady, containerMap.Clone(), containerRunningSet); err != nil {\n   706→\t\treturn err\n   707→\t}\n   708→\n   709→\treturn nil\n   710→}\n   711→\n   712→func (cm *containerManagerImpl) GetPluginRegistrationHandlers() map[string]cache.PluginHandler {\n   713→\tres := map[string]cache.PluginHandler{\n SystemCgroupsLimit() v1.ResourceList {\n   765→\tcpuLimit := int64(0)\n   766→\n   767→\t// Sum up resources of all external containers.\n   768→\tfor _, cont := range cm.systemContainers {\n 775→\t\t\tresource.DecimalSI),\n   776→\t}\n   777→}\n   778→\n   779→func isProcessRunningInHost(logger klog.Logger, pid int) (bool, error) {\n   780→\t// Get init pid namespace.\n   781→\tinitPidNs, err := os.Readlink(\"/proc/1/ns/pid\")\n   782→\tif err != nil {\n   783→\t\treturn false, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to find pid namespace of init process\")\n   784→\t}\n   785→\tlogger.V(10).Info(\"Found init PID namespace\", \"namespace\", initPidNs)\n   786→\tprocessPidNs, err := os.Readlink(fmt.Sprintf(\"/proc/%d/ns/pid\", pid))\n   787→\tif err != nil {\n   788→\t\treturn false, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to find pid namespace of process %q\", pid)\n   789→\t}\n   790→\tlogger.V(10).Info(\"Process info\", \"pid\", pid, \"namespace\", processPidNs)\n   791→\treturn initPidNs == processPidNs, nil\n   792→}\n   793→\n   794→func ensureProcessInContainerWithOOMScore(logger klog.Logger, pid int, oomScoreAdj int, manager cgroups.Manager) error {\n   795→\tif runningInHost, err := isProcessRunningInHost(logger, pid); err != nil {\n   796→\t\t// Err on the side of caution. Avoid moving the docker daemon unless we are able to identify its context.\n   797→\t\treturn err\n   798→\t} else if !runningInHost {\n   799→\t\t// Process is running inside a container. Don't touch that.\n   800→\t\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"PID is not running in the host namespace\", \"pid\", pid)\n   801→\t\treturn nil\n   802→\t}\n   803→\n   804→\tvar errs []error\n   805→\tif manager != nil {\n   806→\t\tcont, err := getContainer(logger, pid)\n   807→\t\tif err != nil {\n   808→\t\t\terrs = append(errs, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to find container of PID %d: %v\", pid, err))\n   809→\t\t}\n   810→\n   811→\t\tname := \"\"\n   812→\t\tcgroups, err := manager.GetCgroups()\n   813→\t\tif err != nil {\n   814→\t\t\terrs = append(errs, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to get cgroups for %d: %v\", pid, err))\n   815→\t\t} else {\n   816→\t\t\tname = cgroups.Name\n   817→\t\t}\n   818→\n   819→\t\tif cont != name {\n   820→\t\t\terr = manager.Apply(pid)\n   821→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   822→\t\t\t\terrs = append(errs, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to move PID %d (in %q) to %q: %v\", pid, cont, name, err))\n   823→\t\t\t}\n   824→\t\t}\n   825→\t}\n   826→\n   827→\t// Also apply oom-score-adj to processes\n   828→\toomAdjuster := oom.NewOOMAdjuster()\n   829→\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Attempting to apply oom_score_adj to process\", \"oomScoreAdj\", oomScoreAdj, \"pid\", pid)\n   830→\tif err := oomAdjuster.ApplyOOMScoreAdj(pid, oomScoreAdj); err != nil {\n   831→\t\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"Failed to apply oom_score_adj to process\", \"oomScoreAdj\", oomScoreAdj, \"pid\", pid, \"err\", err)\n   832→\t\terrs = append(errs, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to apply oom score %d to PID %d: %v\", oomScoreAdj, pid, err))\n   833→\t}\n   834→\treturn utilerrors.NewAggregate(errs)\n   835→}\n   836→\n   837→// getContainer returns the cgroup associated with the specified pid.\n   838→// It enforces a unified hierarchy for memory and cpu cgroups.\n   839→// On systemd environments, it uses the name=systemd cgroup for the specified pid.\n   840→func getContainer(logger klog.Logger, pid int) (string, error) {\n   841→\tcgs, err := cgroups.ParseCgroupFile(fmt.Sprintf(\"/proc/%d/cgroup\", pid))\n   842→\tif err != nil {\n   843→\t\treturn \"\", err\n   844→\t}\n   845→\n   846→\tif cgroups.IsCgroup2UnifiedMode() {\n   847→\t\tc, found := cgs[\"\"]\n   848→\t\tif !found {\n   849→\t\t\treturn \"\", cgroups.NewNotFoundError(\"unified\")\n   850→\t\t}\n   851→\t\treturn c, nil\n   852→\t}\n   853→\n   854→\tcpu, found := cgs[\"cpu\"]\n   855→\tif !found {\n   856→\t\treturn \"\", cgroups.NewNotFoundError(\"cpu\")\n   857→\t}\n   858→\tmemory, found := cgs[\"memory\"]\n   859→\tif !found {\n   860→\t\treturn \"\", cgroups.NewNotFoundError(\"memory\")\n   861→\t}\n   862→\n   863→\t// since we use this container for accounting, we need to ensure its a unified hierarchy.\n   864→\tif cpu != memory {\n   865→\t\treturn \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"cpu and memory cgroup hierarchy not unified.  cpu: %s, memory: %s\", cpu, memory)\n   866→\t}\n   867→\n   868→\t// on systemd, every pid is in a unified cgroup hierarchy (name=systemd as seen in systemd-cgls)\n   869→\t// cpu and memory accounting is off by default, users may choose to enable it per unit or globally.\n   870→\t// users could enable CPU and memory accounting globally via /etc/systemd/system.conf (DefaultCPUAccounting=true DefaultMemoryAccounting=true).\n   871→\t// users could also enable CPU and memory accounting per unit via CPUAccounting=true and MemoryAccounting=true\n   872→\t// we only warn if accounting is not enabled for CPU or memory so as to not break local development flows where kubelet is launched in a terminal.\n   873→\t// for example, the cgroup for the user session will be something like /user.slice/user-X.slice/session-X.scope, but the cpu and memory\n   874→\t// cgroup will be the closest ancestor where accounting is performed (most likely /) on systems that launch docker containers.\n   875→\t// as a result, on those systems, you will not get cpu or memory accounting statistics for kubelet.\n   876→\t// in addition, you would not get memory or cpu accounting for the runtime unless accounting was enabled on its unit (or globally).\n   877→\tif systemd, found := cgs[\"name=systemd\"]; found {\n   878→\t\tif systemd != cpu {\n   879→\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"CPUAccounting not enabled for process\", \"pid\", pid)\n   880→\t\t}\n   881→\t\tif systemd != memory {\n   882→\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"MemoryAccounting not enabled for process\", \"pid\", pid)\n   883→\t\t}\n   884→\t\treturn systemd, nil\n   885→\t}\n   886→\n   887→\treturn cpu, nil\n   888→}\n   889→\n   890→// Ensures the system container is created and all non-kernel threads and process 1\n   891→// without a container are moved to it.\n   892→//\n   893→// The reason of leaving kernel threads at root cgroup is that we don't want to tie the\n   894→// execution of these threads with to-be defined /system quota and create priority inversions.\n   895→func ensureSystemCgroups(logger klog.Logger, rootCgroupPath string, manager cgroups.Manager) error {\n   896→\t// Move non-kernel PIDs to the system container.\n   897→\t// Only keep errors on latest attempt.\n   898→\tvar finalErr error\n   899→\tfor i := 0; i <= 10; i++ {\n   900→\t\tallPids, err := cmutil.GetPids(rootCgroupPath)\n   901→\t\tif err != nil {\n   902→\t\t\tfinalErr = fmt.Errorf(\"failed to list PIDs for root: %v\", err)\n   903→\t\t\tcontinue\n   904→\t\t}\n   905→\n   906→\t\t// Remove kernel pids and other protected PIDs (pid 1, PIDs already in system & kubelet containers)\n   907→\t\tpids := make([]int, 0, len(allPids))\n   908→\t\tfor _, pid := range allPids {\n   909→\t\t\tif pid == 1 || isKernelPid(pid) {\n   910→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   911→\t\t\t}\n   912→\n   913→\t\t\tpids = append(pids, pid)\n   914→\t\t}\n   915→\n   916→\t\t// Check if we have moved all the non-kernel PIDs.\n   917→\t\tif len(pids) == 0 {\n   918→\t\t\treturn nil\n   919→\t\t}\n   920→\n   921→\t\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"Moving non-kernel processes\", \"pids\", pids)\n   922→\t\tfor _, pid := range pids {\n   923→\t\t\terr := manager.Apply(pid)\n   924→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   925→\t\t\t\tname := \"\"\n   926→\t\t\t\tcgroups, err := manager.GetCgroups()\n   927→\t\t\t\tif err == nil {\n   928→\t\t\t\t\tname = cgroups.Name\n   929→\t\t\t\t}\n   930→\n   931→\t\t\t\tfinalErr = fmt.Errorf(\"failed to move PID %d into the system container %q: %v\", pid, name, err)\n   932→\t\t\t}\n   933→\t\t}\n   934→\n   935→\t}\n   936→\n   937→\treturn finalErr\n   938→}\n   939→\n   940→// Determines whether the specified PID is a kernel PID.\n   941→func isKernelPid(pid int) bool {\n   942→\t// Kernel threads have no associated executable.\n   943→\t_, err := os.Readlink(fmt.Sprintf(\"/proc/%d/exe\", pid))\n   944→\treturn err != nil && os.IsNotExist(err)\n   945→}\n   946→\n   947→// GetCapacity returns node capacity data for \"cpu\", \"memory\", \"ephemeral-storage\", and \"huge-pages*\"\n   948→// At present this method is only invoked when introspecting ephemeral storage\n   949→func (cm *containerManagerImpl) GetCapacity(localStorageCapacityIsolation bool) v1.ResourceList {\n   950→\tcm.RLock()\n   951→\tdefer cm.RUnlock()\n   952→\t// Use klog.TODO() because we currently do not have a proper logger to pass in.\n   953→\t// Replace this with an appropriate logger when refactoring this function to accept a logger parameter.\n   954→\tlogger := klog.TODO()\n   955→\tif localStorageCapacityIsolation {\n   956→\t\t// We store allocatable ephemeral-storage in the capacity property once we Start() the container manager\n   957→\t\tif _, ok := cm.capacity[v1.ResourceEphemeralStorage]; !ok {\n   958→\t\t\t// If we haven't yet stored the capacity for ephemeral-storage, we can try to fetch it directly from cAdvisor,\n   959→\t\t\tif cm.cadvisorInterface != nil {\n   960→\t\t\t\trootfs, err := cm.cadvisorInterface.RootFsInfo()\n   961→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   962→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Unable to get rootfs data from cAdvisor interface\")\n   963→\t\t\t\t\t// If the rootfsinfo retrieval from cAdvisor fails for any reason, fallback to returning the capacity property with no ephemeral storage data\n   964→\t\t\t\t\treturn cm.capacity\n   965→\t\t\t\t}\n   966→\t\t\t\t// We don't want to mutate cm.capacity here so we'll manually construct a v1.ResourceList from it,\n   967→\t\t\t\t// and add ephemeral-storage\n   968→\t\t\t\tcapacityWithEphemeralStorage := v1.ResourceList{}\n   969→\t\t\t\tfor rName, rQuant := range cm.capacity {\n   970→\t\t\t\t\tcapacityWithEphemeralStorage[rName] = rQuant\n   971→\t\t\t\t}\n   972→\t\t\t\tcapacityWithEphemeralStorage[v1.ResourceEphemeralStorage] = cadvisor.EphemeralStorageCapacityFromFsInfo(rootfs)[v1.ResourceEphemeralStorage]\n   973→\t\t\t\treturn capacityWithEphemeralStorage\n   974→\t\t\t}\n   975→\t\t}\n   976→\t}\n   977→\treturn cm.capacity\n   978→}\n   979→\n   980→func (cm *containerManagerImpl) GetDevicePluginResourceCapacity() (v1.ResourceList, v1.ResourceList, []string) {\n   981→\treturn cm.deviceManager.GetCapacity()\n   982→}\n   983→\n   984→func (cm *containerManagerImpl) []*podresourcesapi.DynamicResource {\n  1027→\t// Use klog.TODO() because we currently do not have a proper logger to pass in.\n  1028→\t// Replace this with an appropriate logger when refactoring this function to accept a logger parameter.\n  1029→\tlogger := klog.TODO()\n  1030→\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(kubefeatures.DynamicResourceAllocation) {\n  1031→\t\treturn []*podresourcesapi.DynamicResource{}\n  1032→\t}\n  1033→\n  1034→\tvar containerDynamicResources []*podresourcesapi.DynamicResource\n  1035→\tcontainerClaimInfos, err := 203→}\n   204→\n   205→// getQoSMemoryRequests sums and returns the memory request of all pods for\n   206→// guaranteed and burstable qos classes.\n   207→func (m *qosContainerManagerImpl) 233→// setMemoryReserve sums the memory limits of all pods in a QOS class,\n   234→// calculates QOS class memory limits, and set those limits in the\n   235→// CgroupConfig for each QOS class.\n   236→func (m *qosContainerManagerImpl) setMemoryReserve(logger klog.Logger, configs map[v1.PodQOSClass]*CgroupConfig, percentReserve int64) {\n   237→\tqosMemoryRequests := m.getQoSMemoryRequests()\n   238→\n   239→\tresources := m.getNodeAllocatable()\n   240→\tallocatableResource, ok := resources[v1.ResourceMemory]\n   241→\tif !ok {\n   242→\t\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Allocatable memory value could 247→\t\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Allocatable memory reported as 0, might be in standalone mode, not setting QoS memory limits\")\n   248→\t\treturn\n   249→\t}\n   250→\n   251→\tfor qos, limits := range percentReserve / 100)\n   258→\tconfigs[v1.PodQOSBurstable].ResourceParameters.Memory = &burstableLimit\n   259→\tconfigs[v1.PodQOSBestEffort].ResourceParameters.Memory = &bestEffortLimit\n   260→}\n prevent further growth.\n   265→func (m *qosContainerManagerImpl) retrySetMemoryReserve(logger klog.Logger, configs map[v1.PodQOSClass]*CgroupConfig, percentReserve int64) {\n   266→\t// Unreclaimable memory usage may already exceeded the desired limit\n   267→\t// Attempt to set the limit near the current usage to put pressure\n   268→\t// on the cgroup and prevent further growth.\n   269→\tfor 283→\t\t\tconfigs[qos].ResourceParameters.Memory = &usage\n   284→\t\t}\n   285→\t}\n   286→}\n   287→\n   288→// setMemoryQoS sums the memory requests of all pods in the Burstable class,\n   289→// > 0 {\n   308→\t\tif configs[v1.PodQOSGuaranteed].ResourceParameters.Unified == nil {\n   309→\t\t\tconfigs[v1.PodQOSGuaranteed].ResourceParameters.Unified = make(map[string]string)\n   310→\t\t}\n 56→\n    57→// Manager interface provides methods for Kubelet to manage pod topology hints\n    58→type Manager interface {\n    59→\t// PodAdmitHandler is implemented by Manager\n quota is measured in two values:\n    65→\t//  - cfs_period_us=100ms (the amount of time to measure usage across given by period)\n    66→\t//  - cfs_quota=20ms (the amount of cpu time allowed to be MAIN CONTAINER MANAGER (containerManagerImpl) INTEGRATION\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/container_manager_linux.go`\n\nThe `containerManagerImpl` struct is the central orchestrator for all container resource management:\n\n```go\ntype containerManagerImpl struct {\n    sync.RWMutex\n    cadvisorInterface cadvisor.Interface\n    mountUtil         mount.Interface\n    NodeConfig\n    status Status\n    systemContainers []*systemContainer\n    periodicTasks []func()\n    subsystems *CgroupSubsystems\n    nodeInfo   *v1.Node\n    cgroupManager CgroupManager\n    capacity v1.ResourceList\n    internalCapacity v1.ResourceList\n    cgroupRoot CgroupName\n    recorder record.EventRecorder\n    \n    // Sub-managers\n    qosContainerManager QOSContainerManager\n    deviceManager devicemanager.Manager\n    cpuManager cpumanager.Manager\n    memoryManager memorymanager.Manager\n    topologyManager topologymanager.Manager\n    draManager *dra.Manager\n    \n    kubeClient clientset.Interface\n    resourceUpdates chan resourceupdates.Update\n}\n```\n\n**Key Integration Points:**\n\n1. **CPU Manager** - Manages CPU affinity and exclusive CPU allocation\n2. **Memory Manager** - Handles NUMA-aware memory allocation\n3. **Device Manager** - Manages extended resources (GPUs, accelerators)\n4. **DRA Manager** - Dynamic Resource Allocation for ResourceClaims\n5. **Topology Manager** - Coordinates topology affinity across all managers\n6. **QOS Container Manager** - Manages QoS tier cgroups (Guaranteed, Burstable, BestEffort)\n\n---\n\n### 2. MAIN ENTRY POINT AND INITIALIZATION\n\n**Key Function:** `NewContainerManager()` (lines 207-392)\n\n**Initialization Flow:**\n\n1. **Subsystem Detection:**\n   - Gets mounted cgroup subsystems using `GetCgroupSubsystems()`\n   - Validates system requirements (cpu, memory cgroups are mandatory)\n\n2. **Cgroup Manager Creation:**\n   - Creates either `cgroupV1impl` or `cgroupV2impl` based on system\n   - Validates cgroup root path exists\n\n3. **Sub-Manager Initialization (Sequential):**\n   ```\n   a) Topology Manager → NewManager() with machine topology\n   b) Device Manager → NewManagerImpl() with topology hints\n   c) CPU Manager → NewManager() with reserved CPUs\n   d) Memory Manager → NewManager() with memory reservations\n   e) DRA Manager → NewManager() (if feature enabled)\n   f) QOS Container Manager → NewQOSContainerManager()\n   ```\n\n4. **Resource Updates Channel:**\n   - Creates buffered channel: `cm.resourceUpdates = make(chan resourceupdates.Update, 10)`\n   - Fans-in updates from Device Manager and DRA Manager using goroutines\n   - All updates are forwarded to kubelet's main sync loop\n\n**Container Start Function:** `Start()` (lines 615-710)\n\n1. Builds container map from runtime\n2. Initializes DRA Manager\n3. Starts CPU Manager with active pods callback\n4. Starts Memory Manager\n5. Sets up system containers (kernel tuning, OOM scoring)\n6. Starts Device Manager\n7. Launches background tasks for periodic reconciliation\n\n---\n\n### 3. CGROUP MANAGEMENT HIERARCHY\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/cgroup_manager_linux.go` (manager selection)\n\n#### **Cgroup v1 Implementation**\n- **File:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/cgroup_v1_manager_linux.go`\n- **Manager:** `cgroupV1impl`\n- **Key Constants:**\n  ```go\n  const cgroupv1MemLimitFile string = \"memory.limit_in_bytes\"\n  ```\n- **Features:**\n  - Multiple independent subsystems (cpu, memory, cpuset, etc.)\n  - Separate control for each resource\n  - Less efficient NUMA handling\n- **Deprecation Warning:** Flagged as deprecated in container_manager.go with pointer to KEP migration guide\n\n#### **Cgroup v2 Implementation**\n- **File:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/cgroup_v2_manager_linux.go`\n- **Manager:** `cgroupV2impl`\n- **Key Constants:**\n  ```go\n  const (\n      cgroupv2MemLimitFile  = \"memory.max\"\n      cgroupv2CpuMaxFile    = \"cpu.max\"\n      cgroupv2CpuWeightFile = \"cpu.weight\"\n  )\n  ```\n- **Features:**\n  - Unified hierarchy with better resource coordination\n  - Enhanced memory.min/memory.high for memory QoS\n  - Kernel 5.8+ required for root cpu.stat\n\n#### **Cgroup Hierarchy Structure:**\n\n```\n/kubepods (cgroupRoot / defaultNodeAllocatableCgroupName)\n  ├── kubepods.slice (systemd format)\n  │   ├── /guaranteed (Guaranteed QoS pods)\n  │   ├── /burstable (Burstable QoS pods)\n  │   │   └── pod-{UID} (pod-level cgroups)\n  │   │       ├── container1\n  │   │       └── container2\n  │   └── /besteffort (BestEffort QoS pods)\n  │       └── pod-{UID}\n  └── /system (system containers)\n  └── /kubelet (kubelet process cgroup)\n```\n\n#### **System Containers:**\n\n- **System Container** (`SystemCgroupsName`): Runs non-containerized processes\n- **Kubelet Container** (`KubeletCgroupsName`): Confines kubelet process with OOM score adjustment\n- **Periodic Enforcement:** Every 5 minutes to move escaped processes back\n\n---\n\n### 4. KEY FLOW PATHS\n\n#### **A. Pod Admission Flow**\n\n**Interface:** `lifecycle.PodAdmitHandler` (in `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/lifecycle/interfaces.go`)\n\n```go\ntype PodAdmitHandler interface {\n    Admit(attrs *PodAdmitAttributes) PodAdmitResult\n}\n\ntype PodAdmitAttributes struct {\n    Pod *v1.Pod\n    OtherPods []*v1.Pod\n}\n```\n\n**Implementation:** Topology Manager implements this interface\n\n**Flow:**\n1. Kubelet calls `Admit()` during pod acceptance phase\n2. **Topology Manager** (`GetAllocateResourcesPodAdmitHandler()` returns it):\n   - Collects topology hints from all hint providers (CPU, Memory, Device managers)\n   - Evaluates if topology alignment is possible\n   - Returns `PodAdmitResult` with Accept/Reject decision\n3. If admitted, moves to container startup\n4. If rejected, pod is rejected with `TopologyAffinityError`\n\n#### **B. Container Startup Flow**\n\n**Interface:** `InternalContainerLifecycle` (in `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/internal_container_lifecycle.go`)\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```go\ntype internalContainerLifecycleImpl struct {\n    cpuManager      cpumanager.Manager\n    memoryManager   memorymanager.Manager\n    topologyManager topologymanager.Manager\n}\n\nfunc (i *internalContainerLifecycleImpl) PreCreateContainer(\n    logger klog.Logger, pod *v1.Pod, container *v1.Container, \n    containerConfig *runtimeapi.ContainerConfig) error\nfunc (i *internalContainerLifecycleImpl) PreStartContainer(\n    logger klog.Logger, pod *v1.Pod, container *v1.Container, \n    containerID string) error\nfunc (i *internalContainerLifecycleImpl) PostStopContainer(\n    logger klog.Logger, containerID string) error\n```\n\n**Phases:**\n\n1. **PreCreateContainer** (`internal_container_lifecycle_linux.go`):\n   - CPU Manager: Gets CPU affinity from `GetCPUAffinity()` → sets `cpusetCpus`\n   - Memory Manager: Gets NUMA nodes → sets `cpusetMems`\n   - Topology Manager: Not called at this stage\n\n2. **PreStartContainer**:\n   - CPU Manager: `AddContainer()` - records container-to-CPU mapping\n   - Memory Manager: `AddContainer()` - records container-to-memory mapping\n   - Topology Manager: `AddContainer()` - tracks container lifecycle\n\n3. **PostStopContainer**:\n   - Topology Manager: `RemoveContainer()` - cleans up affinity tracking\n   - Other managers handle their own cleanup\n\n#### **C. Resource Allocation Flow**\n\n**Location:** `qos_container_manager_linux.go` (lines 316-392, `UpdateCgroups()` method)\n\n**Periodic Update Interval:** 1 minute (`periodicQOSCgroupUpdateInterval`)\n\n**Flow:**\n1. **CPU Shares Calculation** (`setCPUCgroupConfig()`):\n   - Sums CPU requests from all active Burstable pods\n   - Best Effort always gets `MinShares` (2)\n   - Burstable gets calculated shares: `MilliCPUToShares(burstablePodCPURequest)`\n\n2. **Memory Limits** (`setMemoryReserve()`):\n   - Only if QOSReserved feature enabled\n   - Calculates: `burstableLimit = allocatable - (guaranteed * percentReserve / 100)`\n   - Retries if memory usage exceeds limit\n\n3. **Memory QoS** (`setMemoryQoS()` for cgroup v2):\n   - Sets `memory.min` for burstable and guaranteed tiers\n   - Only if MemoryQoS feature enabled and cgroup v2\n\n4. **Updates Applied:**\n   - Calls `cgroupManager.Update()` for each QoS tier\n   - Huge pages set as unbounded\n\n---\n\n### 5. THE resourceUpdates CHANNEL SYSTEM\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/resourceupdates/updates.go`\n\n**Data Structure:**\n```go\ntype Update struct {\n    PodUIDs []string  // Pod UIDs that need status update\n}\n```\n\n**Implementation Details** (container_manager_linux.go, lines 358-389):\n\n1. **Channel Creation:**\n   - Single buffered channel with capacity 10\n   - Created in `NewContainerManager()`\n\n2. **Fan-In Pattern:**\n   ```go\n   sources := map[string]<-chan resourceupdates.Update{}\n   if cm.deviceManager != nil {\n       sources[\"deviceManager\"] = cm.deviceManager.Updates()\n   }\n   if utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(kubefeatures.DynamicResourceAllocation) \n       && cm.draManager != nil {\n       sources[\"draManager\"] = cm.draManager.Updates()\n   }\n   \n   // Each source gets a goroutine to forward updates\n   for name, ch := range sources {\n       wg.Add(1)\n       go func(name string, c <-chan resourceupdates.Update) {\n           defer wg.Done()\n           for v := range c {\n               logger.V(4).Info(\"Container Manager: forwarding resource update\", \n                   \"source\", name, \"pods\", v.PodUIDs)\n               cm.resourceUpdates <- v\n           }\n       }(name, ch)\n   }\n   \n   // Close channel when all sources are done\n   go func() {\n       wg.Wait()\n       close(cm.resourceUpdates)\n   }()\n   ```\n\n3. **Usage:**\n   - Exposed via `Updates()` method returning `<-chan resourceupdates.Update`\n   - Kubelet's main sync loop consumes updates to reconcile pod status\n   - Triggered when device health changes or DRA resources become unavailable\n\n---\n\n### 6. QOS CONFIGURATION HELPER FUNCTIONS\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/helpers_linux.go`\n\n**Key Constants:**\n```go\nconst (\n    MinShares = 2          // Minimum CPU shares (kernel default for zero)\n    MaxShares = 262144     // Maximum CPU shares\n    SharesPerCPU  = 1024   // Shares equivalent to 1 full CPU\n    MilliCPUToCPU = 1000   // Conversion factor\n    QuotaPeriod = 100000   // Default CFS period (100ms in microseconds)\n    MinQuotaPeriod = 1000  // Minimum CFS period (1ms)\n    MinMilliCPULimit = 10  // Minimum milliCPU limit\n)\n```\n\n**Key Functions:**\n\n1. **MilliCPUToShares(milliCPU int64) uint64**\n   - Converts milliCPU to CPU shares for weighted scheduling\n   - Formula: `(milliCPU * SharesPerCPU) / MilliCPUToCPU`\n   - Clamps to `MinShares`-`MaxShares` range\n   - Zero milliCPU returns `MinShares`\n\n2. **MilliCPUToQuota(milliCPU, period int64) int64**\n   - Converts milliCPU to CFS quota (hard limit)\n   - Formula: `(milliCPU * period) / MilliCPUToCPU`\n   - Respects `CPUCFSQuotaPeriod` feature gate\n   - Minimum quota is `MinQuotaPeriod` (1ms)\n\n3. **HugePageLimits(resourceList v1.ResourceList) map[int64]int64**\n   - Extracts huge page sizes from resource list\n   - Maps size to cumulative limit\n\n4. **ResourceConfigForPod(...) *ResourceConfig**\n   - Calculates resource config for pod cgroup creation\n   - Considers:\n     - Pod CPU/memory requests and limits\n     - EnforceCPULimits flag\n     - MemoryQoS feature gate\n     - PodLevelResources feature gate\n\n---\n\n### 7. PODADMITHANDLER INTERFACE AND IMPLEMENTATIONS\n\n**Primary Implementation:** Topology Manager\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/topologymanager/topology_manager.go`\n\n**Method:** `Admit(attrs *lifecycle.PodAdmitAttributes) lifecycle.PodAdmitResult`\n\n**Admission Process:**\n\n1. **Scope Determination:** Pod-scoped vs Container-scoped\n2. **Hint Collection:**\n   - Calls `GetTopologyHints()` on all registered hint providers\n   - Providers: Device Manager, CPU Manager, Memory Manager\n3. **Hint Aggregation:**\n   - Merges hints based on policy (none, best-effort, restricted)\n   - Checks feasibility\n4. **Decision:**\n   - Returns `PodAdmitResult{Admit: true/false, Reason, Message}`\n   - `TopologyAffinityError` type for rejections\n\n**Other Handlers:**\n- Device Manager may implement its own handlers for resource validation\n- DRA Manager implements pod preparation handlers (not admission, but related)\n\n---\n\n### 8. SYSTEM CONTAINER SETUP\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/container_manager_linux.go` (lines 504-584)\n\n**Process: `setupNode()`**\n\n1. **System Requirements Validation:**\n   - Checks kernel tunables (VM overcommit, panic settings, etc.)\n   - Validates CPU hardcapping support\n\n2. **QOS Container Setup:**\n   - Creates top-level QoS containers if `CgroupsPerQOS` enabled\n   - Creates for Burstable and BestEffort (Guaranteed is root)\n   - Starts QOS manager with periodic updates (1-minute interval)\n\n3. **Node Allocatable Enforcement:**\n   - Creates node allocatable cgroup (`kubepods`)\n   - Enforces resource limits on this cgroup\n   - Handles memory overage with retries\n\n4. **System Containers:**\n   ```go\n   if cm.SystemCgroupsName != \"\" {\n       // Create system container for non-containerized processes\n       cont.ensureStateFunc = func(manager cgroups.Manager) error {\n           return ensureSystemCgroups(logger, \"/\", manager)\n       }\n   }\n   ```\n\n5. **Kubelet Container:**\n   - Moves kubelet process into configured cgroup\n   - Applies OOM score adjustment\n   - If no explicit cgroup, periodic task finds and tracks kubelet's cgroup\n\n6. **Periodic Tasks:**\n   - **For system containers:** Every 1 minute - ensure state (move processes)\n   - **For kubelet location:** Every 5 minutes - update kubelet cgroup location\n\n---\n\n### 9. POD CONTAINER MANAGER (Pod-level Cgroups)\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/pod_container_manager_linux.go`\n\n**Hierarchy Creation:**\n\n```\nQOSContainerName (Guaranteed/Burstable/BestEffort)\n└── podContainerName\n    └── Container processes\n```\n\n**Key Methods:**\n\n1. **EnsureExists(pod)**\n   - Creates pod-level cgroup if doesn't exist\n   - Configures CPU/memory using `ResourceConfigForPod()`\n   - Considers:\n     - `DisableCPUQuotaWithExclusiveCPUs` feature gate\n     - `MemoryQoS` feature gate for cgroup v2\n     - Pod PID limits\n\n2. **GetPodContainerName(pod)**\n   - Determines QoS class of pod\n   - Returns hierarchical cgroup name: `[qosClass, \"pod\" + pod-uid-slug]`\n\n3. **Destroy(podCgroupName)**\n   - Removes pod cgroup\n   - Handles errors gracefully\n\n---\n\n### 10. CGROUP MANAGER INTERFACE\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/types.go`\n\n```go\ntype CgroupManager interface {\n    Create(logger, *CgroupConfig) error\n    Destroy(logger, *CgroupConfig) error\n    Update(logger, *CgroupConfig) error\n    Validate(name CgroupName) error\n    Exists(name CgroupName) bool\n    Name(name CgroupName) string           // Internal → cgroupfs\n    CgroupName(name string) CgroupName     // cgroupfs → Internal\n    Pids(logger, name CgroupName) []int\n    ReduceCPULimits(logger, cgroupName CgroupName) error\n    MemoryUsage(name CgroupName) (int64, error)\n    GetCgroupConfig(name CgroupName, resource v1.ResourceName) (*ResourceConfig, error)\n    SetCgroupConfig(logger, name CgroupName, resourceConfig *ResourceConfig) error\n    Version() int                          // 1 or 2\n}\n```\n\n**Driver Support:**\n- `systemd`: Uses systemd slice hierarchy\n- `cgroupfs`: Direct cgroup filesystem manipulation\n\n---\n\n### 11. TOPOLOGY MANAGER INTEGRATION\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/topologymanager/topology_manager.go`\n\n**Hint Provider Pattern:**\n- Providers implement `GetTopologyHints()` returning NUMA affinity options\n- Manager aggregates hints across providers\n- Policies determine acceptability:\n  - `none`: No topology enforcement\n  - `best-effort`: Prefers aligned allocation but accepts misaligned\n  - `restricted`: Rejects misaligned allocations\n\n**Hint Provider Additions:**\n```go\ncm.topologyManager.AddHintProvider(logger, cm.deviceManager)\ncm.topologyManager.AddHintProvider(logger, cm.cpuManager)\ncm.topologyManager.AddHintProvider(logger, cm.memoryManager)\n```\n\n---\n\n### 12. PLATFORM-SPECIFIC IMPLEMENTATIONS\n\n**Linux:** Full functionality\n- `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/container_manager_linux.go` (main)\n- `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/internal_container_lifecycle_linux.go` (PreCreateContainer with CPU/memory affinities)\n\n**Windows:** Limited functionality\n- `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/container_manager_windows.go`\n- **hierarchical orchestration model** where:\n\n1. **containerManagerImpl** is the central coordinator\n2. **Sub-managers** operate independently but share topology hints\n3. **Topology Manager** acts as a policy arbiter for resource alignment\n4. **QOS tiers** provide resource isolation across pod quality-of-service classes\n5. **Periodic updates** ensure the desired state matches actual cgroup configurations\n6. **Resource updates channel** notifies kubelet of device/claim status changes\n7. **System containers** isolate non-pod workloads from pod execution\n8. **InternalContainerLifecycle** hooks into container creation/destruction for resource configuration\n\nThis design achieves high availability, resource isolation, and optimal NUMA topology affinity MAIN ENTRY POINT AND INITIALIZATION\n\n**Key Function:** `NewContainerManager()` (lines 207-392)\n\n**Initialization Flow:**\n\n1. **Subsystem Detection:**\n   - Gets mounted cgroup subsystems using `GetCgroupSubsystems()`\n   - Validates system requirements (cpu, memory cgroups are mandatory)\n\n2. **Cgroup Manager Creation:**\n   - Creates either `cgroupV1impl` or `cgroupV2impl` based on system\n   - Validates cgroup root path exists\n\n3. **Sub-Manager Initialization (Sequential):**\n   ```\n   a) Topology Manager → NewManager() with machine topology\n   b) Device Manager → NewManagerImpl() with topology hints\n   c) CPU Manager → NewManager() with reserved CPUs\n   d) Memory Manager → NewManager() with memory reservations\n   e) DRA Manager → NewManager() (if feature enabled)\n   f) QOS Container Manager → NewQOSContainerManager()\n   ```\n\n4. **Resource Updates Channel:**\n   - Creates buffered channel: `cm.resourceUpdates = make(chan resourceupdates.Update, 10)`\n   - Fans-in updates from Device Manager and DRA Manager using goroutines\n   - All updates are forwarded to kubelet's main sync loop\n\n**Container Start Function:** `Start()` (lines 615-710)\n\n1. Builds container map from runtime\n2. Initializes DRA Manager\n3. Starts CPU Manager with active pods callback\n4. Starts Memory Manager\n5. Sets up system containers (kernel tuning, OOM scoring)\n6. Starts Device Manager\n7. Launches background tasks for periodic reconciliation\n\n---\n\n### 3. CGROUP MANAGEMENT HIERARCHY\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/cgroup_manager_linux.go` (manager selection)\n\n#### **Cgroup v1 Implementation**\n- **File:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/cgroup_v1_manager_linux.go`\n- **Manager:** `cgroupV1impl`\n- **Key Constants:**\n  ```go\n  const cgroupv1MemLimitFile string = \"memory.limit_in_bytes\"\n  ```\n- **Features:**\n  - Multiple independent subsystems (cpu, memory, cpuset, etc.)\n  - Separate control for each resource\n  - Less efficient NUMA handling\n- **Deprecation Warning:** Flagged as deprecated in container_manager.go with pointer to KEP migration guide\n\n#### **Cgroup v2 Implementation**\n- **File:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/cgroup_v2_manager_linux.go`\n- **Manager:** `cgroupV2impl`\n- **Key Constants:**\n  ```go\n  const (\n      cgroupv2MemLimitFile  = \"memory.max\"\n      cgroupv2CpuMaxFile    = \"cpu.max\"\n      cgroupv2CpuWeightFile = \"cpu.weight\"\n  )\n  ```\n- **Features:**\n  - Unified hierarchy with better resource coordination\n  - Enhanced memory.min/memory.high for memory QoS\n  - Kernel 5.8+ required for root cpu.stat\n\n#### **Cgroup Hierarchy Structure:**\n\n```\n/kubepods (cgroupRoot / defaultNodeAllocatableCgroupName)\n  ├── kubepods.slice (systemd format)\n  │   ├── /guaranteed (Guaranteed QoS pods)\n  │   ├── /burstable (Burstable QoS pods)\n  │   │   └── pod-{UID} (pod-level cgroups)\n  │   │       ├── container1\n  │   │       └── container2\n  │   └── /besteffort (BestEffort QoS pods)\n  │       └── pod-{UID}\n  └── /system (system containers)\n  └── /kubelet (kubelet process cgroup)\n```\n\n#### **System Containers:**\n\n- **System Container** (`SystemCgroupsName`): Runs non-containerized processes\n- **Kubelet Container** (`KubeletCgroupsName`): Confines kubelet process with OOM score adjustment\n- **Periodic Enforcement:** Every 5 minutes to move escaped processes back\n\n---\n\n### 4. KEY FLOW PATHS\n\n#### **A. Pod Admission Flow**\n\n**Interface:** `lifecycle.PodAdmitHandler` (in `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/lifecycle/interfaces.go`)\n\n```go\ntype PodAdmitHandler interface {\n    Admit(attrs *PodAdmitAttributes) PodAdmitResult\n}\n\ntype PodAdmitAttributes struct {\n    Pod *v1.Pod\n    OtherPods []*v1.Pod\n}\n```\n\n**Implementation:** Topology Manager implements this interface\n\n**Flow:**\n1. Kubelet calls `Admit()` during pod acceptance phase\n2. **Topology Manager** (`GetAllocateResourcesPodAdmitHandler()` returns it):\n   - Collects topology hints from all hint providers (CPU, Memory, Device managers)\n   - Evaluates if topology alignment is possible\n   - Returns `PodAdmitResult` with Accept/Reject decision\n3. If admitted, moves to container startup\n4. If rejected, pod is rejected with `TopologyAffinityError`\n\n#### **B. Container Startup Flow**\n\n**Interface:** `InternalContainerLifecycle` (in `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/internal_container_lifecycle.go`)\n\n**Implementation:**\n\n```go\ntype internalContainerLifecycleImpl struct {\n    cpuManager      cpumanager.Manager\n    memoryManager   memorymanager.Manager\n    topologyManager topologymanager.Manager\n}\n\nfunc (i *internalContainerLifecycleImpl) PreCreateContainer(\n    logger klog.Logger, pod *v1.Pod, container *v1.Container, \n    containerConfig *runtimeapi.ContainerConfig) error\nfunc (i *internalContainerLifecycleImpl) PreStartContainer(\n    logger klog.Logger, pod *v1.Pod, container *v1.Container, \n    containerID string) error\nfunc (i *internalContainerLifecycleImpl) PostStopContainer(\n    logger klog.Logger, containerID string) error\n```\n\n**Phases:**\n\n1. **PreCreateContainer** (`internal_container_lifecycle_linux.go`):\n   - CPU Manager: Gets CPU affinity from `GetCPUAffinity()` → sets `cpusetCpus`\n   - Memory Manager: Gets NUMA nodes → sets `cpusetMems`\n   - Topology Manager: Not called at this stage\n\n2. **PreStartContainer**:\n   - CPU Manager: `AddContainer()` - records container-to-CPU mapping\n   - Memory Manager: `AddContainer()` - records container-to-memory mapping\n   - Topology Manager: `AddContainer()` - tracks container lifecycle\n\n3. **PostStopContainer**:\n   - Topology Manager: `RemoveContainer()` - cleans up affinity tracking\n   - Other managers handle their own cleanup\n\n#### **C. POD CONTAINER MANAGER (Pod-level Cgroups)\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/pod_container_manager_linux.go`\n\n**Hierarchy Creation:**\n\n```\nQOSContainerName (Guaranteed/Burstable/BestEffort)\n└── podContainerName\n    └── Container processes\n```\n\n**Key Methods:**\n\n1. **EnsureExists(pod)**\n   - Creates pod-level cgroup if doesn't exist\n   - Configures CPU/memory using `ResourceConfigForPod()`\n   - Considers:\n     - `DisableCPUQuotaWithExclusiveCPUs` feature gate\n     - `MemoryQoS` feature gate for cgroup v2\n     - Pod PID limits\n\n2. **GetPodContainerName(pod)**\n   - Determines QoS class of pod\n   - Returns hierarchical cgroup name: `[qosClass, \"pod\" + pod-uid-slug]`\n\n3. **Destroy(podCgroupName)**\n   - Removes pod cgroup\n   - Handles errors gracefully\n\n---\n\n### 10. CGROUP MANAGER INTERFACE\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/types.go`\n\n```go\ntype CgroupManager interface {\n    Create(logger, *CgroupConfig) error\n    Destroy(logger, *CgroupConfig) error\n    Update(logger, *CgroupConfig) error\n    Validate(name CgroupName) error\n    Exists(name CgroupName) bool\n    Name(name CgroupName) string           // Internal → cgroupfs\n    CgroupName(name string) CgroupName     // cgroupfs → Internal\n    Pids(logger, name CgroupName) []int\n    ReduceCPULimits(logger, cgroupName CgroupName) error\n    MemoryUsage(name CgroupName) (int64, error)\n    GetCgroupConfig(name CgroupName, resource v1.ResourceName) (*ResourceConfig, error)\n    SetCgroupConfig(logger, name CgroupName, resourceConfig *ResourceConfig) error\n    Version() int                          // 1 or 2\n}\n```\n\n**Driver Support:**\n- `systemd`: Uses systemd slice hierarchy\n- `cgroupfs`: Direct cgroup filesystem manipulation\n\n---\n\n### 11. TOPOLOGY MANAGER INTEGRATION\n\n**Location:** `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/topologymanager/topology_manager.go`\n\n**Hint Provider Pattern:**\n- Providers implement `GetTopologyHints()` returning NUMA affinity options\n- Manager aggregates hints across providers\n- Policies determine acceptability:\n  - `none`: No topology enforcement\n  - `best-effort`: Prefers aligned allocation but accepts misaligned\n  - `restricted`: Rejects misaligned allocations\n\n**Hint Provider Additions:**\n```go\ncm.topologyManager.AddHintProvider(logger, cm.deviceManager)\ncm.topologyManager.AddHintProvider(logger, cm.cpuManager)\ncm.topologyManager.AddHintProvider(logger, cm.memoryManager)\n```\n\n---\n\n### 12. PLATFORM-SPECIFIC IMPLEMENTATIONS\n\n**Linux:** Full functionality\n- `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/container_manager_linux.go` (main)\n- `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/internal_container_lifecycle_linux.go` (PreCreateContainer with CPU/memory affinities)\n\n**Windows:** Limited functionality\n- `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/container_manager_windows.go`\n- `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/internal_container_lifecycle_windows.go`\n- No cgroup support, basic resource limits only\n\n**Unsupported Platforms:** Stub implementations\n- `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/container_manager_unsupported.go`\n- `/workspace/pkg/kubelet/cm/internal_container_lifecycle_unsupported.go`\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nThe container manager subsystem uses a **hierarchical orchestration model** where:\n\n1. **containerManagerImpl** is the central coordinator\n2. **Sub-managers** operate independently but share topology hints\n3. **Topology Manager** acts as a policy arbiter for resource alignment\n4. **QOS tiers** provide resource isolation across pod quality-of-service classes\n5. **Periodic updates** ensure the desired state matches actual cgroup configurations\n6. **Resource updates channel** notifies kubelet of device/claim status changes\n7. **System containers** isolate non-pod workloads from pod execution\n8. **InternalContainerLifecycle** hooks into container creation/destruction for resource configuration\n\nThis design achieves high availability, resource isolation, and optimal NUMA topology affinity while maintaining backward compatibility with cgroup v1 and forward compatibility with cgroup v2."}],"totalDurationMs":78816,"totalTokens":77302,"totalToolUseCount":31,"usage":{"input_tokens":6,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2829,"cache_read_input_tokens":69141,"output_tokens":5326,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2829,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"}}}
